<td style="width:12%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;5.03</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Amendments to Articles of Incorporation or Bylaws; Change in Fiscal Year.</td></tr></table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Effective on October&#160;9, 2019, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) amended and restated its existing bylaws (the &#8220;Restated Bylaws&#8221;). The amendments include:</p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">

<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">an amendment to Article III, Section&#160;9 to allow the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) or any committee thereof to act by written consent by submitting such consent through electronic transmission;</td></tr></table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">

<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">an amendment to Article V to allow the Board to delegate to the Chief Executive Officer or President the power to appoint and remove other officers; and</td></tr></table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">

<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>

<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">

<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">notices for meetings of stockholders, convening and adjourning such meetings and the posting of the stockholder list for such meetings;</td></tr></table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">

<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">

<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">notices for special meetings of the Board;</td></tr></table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">

<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">

<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
